Compute the matrix of the (weighted) L2-\/product for the cell of index iT. The stabilisation here is based on cell and face potentials. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em iT} & index of the cell \\
\hline
{\em penalty\+\_\+factor} & pre-\/factor for stabilisation term \\
\hline
{\em mass\+\_\+\+Pk3\+\_\+T} & if pre-\/computed, the mass matrix of (P$^\wedge$k(T))$^\wedge$3; if none is pre-\/computed, passing Eigen\+::\+Matrix\+Xd\+::\+Zero(1,1) will force the calculation \\
\hline
{\em weight} & weight function in the L2 product, defaults to 1 \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Eigen\+::\+Vector\+Xd SXGrad\+::interpolate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{group__DDRCore_gad31e6bd58000471db0da65d94f2e0c30}{Function\+Type}} \&}]{q,  }\item[{const int}]{doe\+\_\+cell = {\ttfamily -\/1},  }\item[{const int}]{doe\+\_\+face = {\ttfamily -\/1},  }\item[{const int}]{doe\+\_\+edge = {\ttfamily -\/1} }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}



Interpolator of a continuous function. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em q} & The function to interpolate \\
\hline
{\em doe\+\_\+cell} & The optional degre of cell quadrature rules to compute the interpolate. If negative, then 2$\ast$degree()+3 will be used. \\
\hline
{\em doe\+\_\+face} & The optional degre of face quadrature rules to compute the interpolate. If negative, then 2$\ast$degree()+3 will be used. \\
\hline
{\em doe\+\_\+edge} & The optional degre of edge quadrature rules to compute the interpolate. If negative, then 2$\ast$degree()+3 will be used. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily Eigen\+::\+Vector\+Xd XGrad\+::interpolate (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{group__DDRCore_ga433efca9d7ce661d4bc9e5386d131cf8}{Function\+Type}} \&}]{q,  }\item[{const int}]{doe\+\_\+cell = {\ttfamily -\/1},  }\item[{const int}]{doe\+\_\+face = {\ttfamily -\/1},  }\item[{const int}]{doe\+\_\+edge = {\ttfamily -\/1} }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const}



Interpolator of a continuous function. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
